##########
#  ＷＷ２日本降伏判定
##########

# 対米降伏

event = {
	id = 131500
	random = no
	country = JAP

	trigger = {
		war = { country = JAP country = USA }
		NOT = {
			alliance = { country = JAP country = ENG }
			alliance = { country = USA country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = JAP country = SOV }
			control = { province = 1184 data = SOV } # 東京がソ連の支配下でない(対ソ降伏条件)
		}
		OR = {
			event = 131596
			AND = { # 東京・大阪・名古屋失陥 #FEPKBETA4
				NOT = {
				#	control = { province = 1178 data = JAP } # 旭川
				#	control = { province = 1179 data = JAP } # 札幌
				#	control = { province = 1180 data = JAP } # 仙台
				#	control = { province = 1181 data = JAP } # 秋田
				#	control = { province = 1182 data = JAP } # 福岡
				#	control = { province = 1183 data = JAP } # 新潟
					control = { province = 1184 data = JAP } # 東京
					control = { province = 1185 data = JAP } # 名古屋
				#	control = { province = 1186 data = JAP } # 金沢
					control = { province = 1187 data = JAP } # 大阪
				#	control = { province = 1188 data = JAP } # 広島
				#	control = { province = 1189 data = JAP } # 四国
				#	control = { province = 1190 data = JAP } # 福岡
				#	control = { province = 1191 data = JAP } # 鹿児島
				}
			}
			AND = { # 対米単独戦争時、中核州80％失陥
				lost_national = { country = JAP value = 80 }
				NOT = {
					war = { country = JAP country = SOV }
				}
			}
			AND = { # ソ連参戦時、満州消滅かつ中核州30％失陥
				lost_national = { country = JAP value = 30 }
				NOT = {
					exists = MAN
				}
				war = { country = JAP country = SOV }
			}
			AND = { # ソ連参戦時、中核州60％失陥
				lost_national = { country = JAP value = 60 }
				war = { country = JAP country = SOV }
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			ispuppet = USA #BETA修正パッチ
		}
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
	offset = 3
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_131500_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_131500_DESC"

	picture = "JAP_surrender"

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_131500_ACTA"
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = trigger which = 131505 } #USA
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "EVT_131500_ACTB"
		ai_chance = 0
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 1 }
		command = { type = dissent value = 10 }
	}
}

#対ソ降伏

event = {
	id = 131501
	random = no
	country = JAP

	trigger = {
		war = { country = JAP country = SOV }
		control = { province = 1184 data = SOV } # 東京がソ連の支配下(対ソ降伏条件)
		NOT = {
			alliance = { country = JAP country = ENG }
			alliance = { country = USA country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = JAP country = USA }
		}
		OR = {
			AND = { # 名古屋・大阪失陥 #FEPKBETA4
				NOT = {
				#	control = { province = 1178 data = JAP } # 旭川
				#	control = { province = 1179 data = JAP } # 札幌
				#	control = { province = 1180 data = JAP } # 仙台
				#	control = { province = 1181 data = JAP } # 秋田
				#	control = { province = 1182 data = JAP } # 福岡
				#	control = { province = 1183 data = JAP } # 新潟
				#	control = { province = 1184 data = JAP } # 東京
					control = { province = 1185 data = JAP } # 名古屋
				#	control = { province = 1186 data = JAP } # 金沢
					control = { province = 1187 data = JAP } # 大阪
				#	control = { province = 1188 data = JAP } # 広島
				#	control = { province = 1189 data = JAP } # 四国
				#	control = { province = 1190 data = JAP } # 福岡
				#	control = { province = 1191 data = JAP } # 鹿児島
				}
			}
			AND = { # 対ソ単独戦争時、中核州80％失陥
				lost_national = { country = JAP value = 80 }
				NOT = {
					war = { country = JAP country = USA }
				}
			}
			AND = { # 米国または連合国参戦時、満州消滅・朝鮮失陥かつ中核州30％失陥
				lost_national = { country = JAP value = 30 }
				NOT = {
					exists = MAN
					control = { province = 1194 data = JAP }#以下朝鮮半島
					control = { province = 1195 data = JAP }
					control = { province = 1196 data = JAP }
					control = { province = 1197 data = JAP }
					control = { province = 1198 data = JAP }
					control = { province = 1199 data = JAP }
					control = { province = 1200 data = JAP }
					control = { province = 1201 data = JAP }
					control = { province = 1376 data = JAP }
					control = { province = 1391 data = JAP }
					control = { province = 1392 data = JAP }
					control = { province = 1393 data = JAP }
				}
				war = { country = JAP country = USA }
			}
			AND = { # 米国参戦時、中核州60％失陥
				lost_national = { country = JAP value = 60 }
				war = { country = JAP country = USA }
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			ispuppet = SOV #BETA修正パッチ
		}
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
	offset = 3
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_131501_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_131501_DESC"

	picture = "JAP_surrender"

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_131501_ACTA"
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = trigger which = 131506 } # SOV
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "EVT_131501_ACTB"
		ai_chance = 0
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 1 }
		command = { type = dissent value = 10 }
	}
}


# 対独降伏

event = {
	id = 131502
	random = no
	country = JAP

	trigger = {
		war = { country = JAP country = GER }
		OR = {
			AND = {	#連合日本で、中核州の80％を損失
				alliance = { country = ENG country = JAP }
				lost_national = { country = JAP value = 80 }
				NOT = { event = 131002 }
			}
			AND = {	#米国に降伏したあとで、米英が降伏済み且つ中核州の10％を損失
				event = 131500	#日本対米降伏
				OR = {
					event = 131231	#米国対独降伏
					ispuppet = USA
				}
				event = 131002	#英国対独降伏
				lost_national = { country = JAP value = 10 }
			}
			AND = {	#ソ連に降伏したあとで、ソ連がビタピ済み且つ中核州の30％を損失
				event = 131501	#日本対ソ降伏
				event = 135302	#ビタピ（日本中立）
				lost_national = { country = JAP value = 30 }
			}
			AND = {	#単独参戦で、米英ソが全てドイツと非戦で、中核州の80％を損失
				lost_national = { country = JAP value = 60 }
				NOT = { alliance = { country = ENG country = JAP } }
				NOT = { alliance = { country = USA country = JAP } }
				NOT = { war = { country = ENG country = GER } }
				NOT = { war = { country = USA country = GER } }
				NOT = { war = { country = SOV country = GER } }
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			ispuppet = GER #BETA修正パッチ
		}
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
	offset = 3
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_131502_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_131502_DESC"

	picture = "JAP_surrender"

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_131502_ACTA"
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = trigger which = 131507 } #GER
	}
	action_b = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				event = 131500
				event = 131501
			}
		}
		name = "EVT_131502_ACTB"
		ai_chance = 0
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 1 }
		command = { type = dissent value = 10 }
	}
}

#id = 131503-4 free

	id = 131505 # trigger 131500
	random = no
	country = USA

	name = "EVT_131505_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_131505_DESC"

	action_a = {

		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = trigger which = 131510 }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 131501 }#surrender to SOV
		command = { type = dissent value = -15 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "EVT_131505_ACTB"
		ai_chance = 0
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 1 }
		command = { type = dissent value = 15 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 131613
	country = VIE
	random = no

	trigger = {
		event = 131612 # 明号作戦発動済み
	}

	name = "EVT_57110_NAME" # ベトナム帝国独立宣言
	desc = "EVT_57110_DESC" # 

# バオ・ダイ帝は甲申条約を破棄し、フランスからの独立と日本との協働を宣言した。
# 首相に著名な文人であったチャン・チョン・キムを任命し、内閣を組織させた。
# フランス式の町名をアンナンの町名に復し、フランス人の官僚を免官して、フランス人の銅像を次々と撤去した。
# また、中等教育における教授言語をフランス語からベトナム語に改定し、その後の教育制度に大きな影響を与えている。
# しかしその後の大飢饉や日本によるフランスの資産保護政策により、ホー・チ・ミンに攻撃材料を与えてしまった。
# カンボジアとの間に領土紛争を抱え、ラオスとも民族をめぐる紛争を抱えた。
# さらに史実では４か月後に日本のポツダム宣言受託を受け、ベトナム帝国は消滅する事になる。

	picture = "VIC"
	style = 0
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1934 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_57110_ACTA" # 前途多難である…

		command = { type = access which = JAP } # 軍の通行許可
		command = { type = dissent value = 15 } # 国民不満度 +15
	}
}

event = {
	id = 131619
	country = JAP
	random = no

	trigger = {
		not = { exists = PHI } # フィリピンが存在しない
		control = { province = 1737 data = -3 } # マニラ
	}

	name = "EVT_57116_NAME" # フィリピン第二共和国の成立
	desc = "EVT_57116_DESC" # 

# 1899年にフィリピンがアメリカとの戦争に敗れて以来、アルテミオ・リカルテ将軍は日本に亡命するなど日本はフィリピンの独立を支援していた。
# 太平洋戦争が勃発し日本軍がフィリピンを完全に制圧すると、抗日ゲリラ運動や軍票の乱発などの政策の失敗から窮乏化を招き、
# 日本は民心を回復させるためにホセ・ラウレルを大統領とするフィリピン第二共和国の独立を認めた。
# 1943年11月5日に東京で開かれた大東亜会議に独立国家として参加したが、ラウレル政権は民衆の支持を得ることはできなかった。
# 後にラウレル政権も日本との対決姿勢を強めたため、日本はリカルテをはじめとする独立運動家達によって設立されたフィリピン愛国連盟を支援した。

	picture = "Indochina_demand"
	style = 0
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1934 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action_a = {
		ai_chance = 97
		name = "EVT_57116_ACTA" # 独立宣言をさせる
		command = { type = dissent value = -2 } # 国民不満度 -2
		command = { type = independence which = PHI value = 1 when = 0 } # フィリピン独立
		command = { type = alliance which = PHI } # 
		command = { type = belligerence which = JAP value = -10 } # 日本の好戦度 -10
		command = { type = trigger which = 131620 } # フィリピン第二共和国の成立 (フィリピン側)
	}
	action_b = {
		ai_chance = 3
		name = "EVT_57116_ACTB" # 完全制圧する
		command = { type = belligerence which = JAP value = 5 } # 日本の好戦性 +5
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 131620 } # フィリピン第二共和国の成立 (フィリピン側)
	}
}

event = {
	id = 131622
	country = JAP
	random = no

	trigger = {
		not = { exists = BUR } # ビルマが存在しない
		control = { province = 1299 data = JAP } # ラングーン
		NOT = { control = { province = 1287 data = -2 } } # インパール	#DHSA0.2
		NOT = { control = { province = 1878 data = -2 } } # レド #BETA修正パッチ
	}

	name = "EVT_57119_NAME" # インパール作戦
	desc = "EVT_57119_DESC" # 

# 日本は日中戦争が膠着すると、援蒋ルートと呼ばれる連合国による中華民国支援のための輸送ルートを遮断するためにビルマに進軍した。
# 1942年にビルマ全土を制圧すると一旦は遮断に成功するものの、44年に入り制空権を失うとビルマ北部のゲリラ部隊への空輸によって
# 再び中国軍と連合国との連携が再開されてしまった。
# 日本軍はインパールを攻略する事で再びこれを遮断するウ号作戦が牟田口司令官により立案され、実行に移された。
# 史実では度重なるインパール攻略の失敗からアウンサン率いるビルマ国民軍はクーデターを起こし、イギリスに寝返ったが
# 日本軍の優勢によってインパールの攻略に成功し、ここにビルマ国の安定が確立した。

	picture = "mutaguchi"
	style = 0
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1934 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action_a = {
		ai_chance = 97
		name = "EVT_57119_ACTA" # 独立宣言をさせる
		command = { type = removeclaim which = 1304 }
		command = { type = dissent value = -2 } # 国民不満度 -2
		command = { type = independence which = BUR value = 1 when = 0 } # ビルマ独立
		command = { type = alliance which = BUR } # 
		command = { type = belligerence which = JAP value = -10 } # 日本の好戦度 -10
		command = { type = trigger which = 131623 } # ビルマ国成立 (ビルマ側)
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U87 value = 1294 } #中国―ミャンマー国境地帯譲渡 # FEPK変更部分 # 1.08
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = U87 value = 1305 }
	}
	action_b = {
		ai_chance = 3
		name = "EVT_57119_ACTB" # 完全制圧する
		command = { type = belligerence which = JAP value = 5 } # 日本の好戦性 +5
		command = { type = removeclaim which = 1304 }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 131623 } # ビルマ国成立 (ビルマ側)
	}
}

#中国南京政府が結構ビルマを落としてしまうことに気づいたので対策
event = {
	id = 131625
	tag = { U87 SIA }	#拡張できるようにしておく
	random = no
	persistent = yes
	trigger = {
		puppet = { country = -1 country = JAP }
		#"North Burma","Burma"
		OR = {
			area = { area = "North Burma" country = -1 value = 1 }
			area = { area = "Burma" country = -1 value = 1 }
		}
		NOT = { exists = BUR }
	}
	
	name = "EVT_131625_NAME"	#占領地の調整
	desc = "EVT_131625_DESC"	#日本が連合国との戦闘に入ると、我が軍も英領インドに対する戦線を展開することを余儀なくされた。幸運にも連合軍の抵抗は大きくなく、ほどなくして我々は全ビルマを制圧することに成功した。我が国が日本の属国で外交権を制限されている以上、我々は彼らにこの地域を割譲せざるを得ない。

	picture = "mutaguchi"
	style = 0

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1934 }
	offset = 5
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }
	
	action = {
		ai_chance = 100
		name = "EVT_131625_ACTA"	#仕方があるまい
		command = { type = secedearea which = JAP value = "North Burma" }
		command = { type = secedearea which = JAP value = "Burma" }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1304 where = JAP }
	}
}

	random = no
	country = GER

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				control = { province = 1728 data = GER } #Canberra
				OR = {
					lost_national = { country = AST value = 75 }
					lost_IC = { country = AST value = 75 }
					lost_VP = { country = AST value = 75 }
				}
			}
		}
		war = { country = AST country = GER }
	}

        date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
        offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_131640_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_131640_DESC"

	picture = "british_reinforcments5"

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_131640_ACTA"
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 131641 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "EVT_131640_ACTB"
		ai_chance = 0
		command = { type = dissent value = 3 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 131660
	random = no
	country = GER

	trigger = { #beaten by force #FEPKBETA1.1
		OR = {	#英国がカナダ臨時政府モードである場合、オタワの領有状況は考慮「しない」
			AND = {
				NOT = { flag = ottawa }
				control = { province = 588 data = GER } #Ottawa
			}
			flag = ottawa
		}
		OR = {
			lost_national = { country = CAN value = 75 }
			lost_IC = { country = CAN value = 75 }
			lost_VP = { country = CAN value = 75 }
			event = 131232 #USA surrenders to germany
			event = 131252 #USA surrenders to axis	#遠藤マイクロ
		}
		war = { country = CAN country = GER }
	}

        date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
        offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }
